<Tag slot="tag">

<TagTitle slot="title">

# Client Search Endpoints

</TagTitle>

</Tag>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/adminsearch [#operation-adminsearch]

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Search the index (admin)_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Retrieves results for search query without respect for permissions. This is available only to privileged users.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationRequestBodySection slot="request-body">

<Section>

<SectionTitle slot="title">

### Request Body [#operation-adminsearch_request]

</SectionTitle>

<SectionContent slot="content">

<OperationRequestBodyDescriptionSection slot="request-body-description">

Admin search request

</OperationRequestBodyDescriptionSection>

  expandByDefault={true}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### cursor [#operation-adminsearch_request_cursor]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Pagination cursor. A previously received opaque token representing the position in the overall results at which to start.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

##### disableSpellcheck [#operation-adminsearch_request_disablespellcheck]

##### inputDetails [#operation-adminsearch_request_inputdetails]

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="inputDetails_hasCopyPaste"
  headingId="operation-adminsearch_request_inputdetails_hascopypaste"
  parentId="inputDetails"

  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### hasCopyPaste [#operation-adminsearch_request_inputdetails_hascopypaste]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Whether the associated query was at least partially copy-pasted.  If subsequent requests are issued after a copy-pasted query is constructed (e.g. with facet modifications), this bit should continue to be set for those requests.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="maxSnippetSize"
  headingId="operation-adminsearch_request_maxsnippetsize"
  typeInfo={{"label":"integer","linkedLabel":"integer","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={true}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### maxSnippetSize [#operation-adminsearch_request_maxsnippetsize]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Hint to the server about how many characters long a snippet may be. Server may return less or more.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
400
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="pageSize"
  headingId="operation-adminsearch_request_pagesize"
  typeInfo={{"label":"integer","linkedLabel":"integer","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={true}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### pageSize [#operation-adminsearch_request_pagesize]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Hint to the server about how many results to send back. Server may return less or more. Structured results and clustered results don't count towards pageSize.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
100
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="query"
  headingId="operation-adminsearch_request_query"
  typeInfo={{"label":"string","linkedLabel":"string","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[{"title":"required","variant":"warning"}]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={true}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### query [#operation-adminsearch_request_query]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

The search terms.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
vacation policy
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="requestOptions_datasourceFilter"
  headingId="operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_datasourcefilter"
  parentId="requestOptions"
  typeInfo={{"label":"string","linkedLabel":"string","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### datasourceFilter [#operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_datasourcefilter]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Filter results to a single datasource name (e.g. gmail, slack). All results are returned if missing.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="requestOptions_datasourcesFilter"
  headingId="operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_datasourcesfilter"
  parentId="requestOptions"
  typeInfo={{"label":"array","linkedLabel":"string","children":[{"label":"string","linkedLabel":"string","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### datasourcesFilter [#operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_datasourcesfilter]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Filter results to one or more datasources (e.g. gmail, slack). All results are returned if missing.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="requestOptions_defaultFacets"
  headingId="operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_defaultfacets"
  parentId="requestOptions"
  typeInfo={{"label":"array","linkedLabel":"string","children":[{"label":"string","linkedLabel":"string","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### defaultFacets [#operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_defaultfacets]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Facets for which FacetResults should be fetched and that don't apply to a particular datasource. If specified, these values will replace the standard default facets (last_updated_at, from, etc.). The requested facets will be returned alongside datasource-specific facets if searching a single datasource.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="requestOptions_disableQueryAutocorrect"
  headingId="operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_disablequeryautocorrect"
  parentId="requestOptions"
  typeInfo={{"label":"boolean","linkedLabel":"boolean","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### disableQueryAutocorrect [#operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_disablequeryautocorrect]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Disables automatic adjustment of the input query for spelling corrections or other reasons.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="requestOptions_exclusions_containerSpecs"
  headingId="operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_exclusions_containerspecs"
  parentId="requestOptions_exclusions"
  typeInfo={{"label":"array","linkedLabel":"union","children":[{"label":"union","linkedLabel":"union","children":[{"label":"","linkedLabel":"<a href=\"#operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_exclusions_containerspecs\"></a>","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}},{"label":"","linkedLabel":"<a href=\"#operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_exclusions_containerspecs\"></a>","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}},{"label":"","linkedLabel":"<a href=\"#operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_exclusions_containerspecs\"></a>","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}},{"label":"","linkedLabel":"<a href=\"#operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_exclusions_containerspecs\"></a>","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### containerSpecs [#operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_exclusions_containerspecs]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Specifications for containers that should be used as part of the restriction (include/exclude). Memberships are recursively defined for a subset of datasources (currently: SharePoint, OneDrive, Google Drive, and Confluence). Please contact the Glean team to enable this for more datasources. Recursive memberships do not apply for Collections.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="requestOptions_facetFilterSets"
  headingId="operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_facetfiltersets"
  parentId="requestOptions"
  typeInfo={{"label":"array","linkedLabel":"<a href=\"#operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_facetfiltersets_facetfilterset\">FacetFilterSet</a>","children":[{"label":"FacetFilterSet","linkedLabel":"<a href=\"#operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_facetfiltersets_facetfilterset\">FacetFilterSet</a>","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### facetFilterSets [#operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_facetfiltersets]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A list of facet filter sets that will be OR'ed together. SearchRequestOptions where both facetFilterSets and facetFilters set are considered as bad request. Callers should set only one of these fields.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableBreakout
  slot="entry"
  id="requestOptions_facetFilterSets_FacetFilterSet"
  headingId="operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_facetfiltersets_facetfilterset"
  parentId="requestOptions_facetFilterSets"
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandableBreakoutTitle slot="title">

#### FacetFilterSet [#operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_facetfiltersets_facetfilterset]

</ExpandableBreakoutTitle>

<ExpandableBreakoutDescription slot="description">

Within a single FacetFilterSet, the filters are treated as AND. For example, owner Sumeet and type Spreadsheet shows documents that are by Sumeet AND are Spreadsheets.

</ExpandableBreakoutDescription>

<ExpandableBreakoutExamples slot="examples">

</ExpandableBreakoutExamples>

<ExpandableBreakoutDefaultValue slot="defaultValue">

</ExpandableBreakoutDefaultValue>

##### facetFilters [#operation-adminsearch_request_requestoptions_facetfilters]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

Recursive memberships do not apply for Collections.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

  typeInfo={{"label":"string","linkedLabel":"string","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### groupName [#operation-adminsearch_responses_200_application-json_rewrittenfacetfilters_facetfilter_groupname]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Indicates the value of a facet, if any, that the given facet is grouped under. This is only used for nested facets, for example, fieldName could be owner and groupName would be Spreadsheet if showing all owners for spreadsheets as a nested facet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
Spreadsheet
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### values [#operation-adminsearch_responses_200_application-json_rewrittenfacetfilters_facetfilter_values]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Within a single FacetFilter, the values are to be treated like an OR. For example, fieldName type with values [EQUALS Presentation, EQUALS Spreadsheet] means we want to show a document if it's a Presentation OR a Spreadsheet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/autocomplete [#operation-autocomplete]

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Autocomplete_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Retrieve query suggestions, operators and documents for the given partially typed query.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/feed [#operation-feed]

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Feed of documents and events_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

The personalized feed/home includes different types of contents including suggestions, recents, calendar events and many more.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationRequestBodySection slot="request-body">

<Section>

<SectionTitle slot="title">

### Request Body [#operation-feed_request]

</SectionTitle>

<SectionContent slot="content">

<OperationRequestBodyDescriptionSection slot="request-body-description">

Includes request params, client data and more for making user's feed.

</OperationRequestBodyDescriptionSection>

<ExpandableSection>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="categories"

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/recommendations [#operation-recommendations]

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Recommend documents_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Retrieve recommended documents for the given URL or Glean Document ID.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/search [#operation-search]

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Search_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Retrieve results from the index for the given query and filters.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationRequestBodySection slot="request-body">

<Section>

<SectionTitle slot="title">

### Request Body [#operation-search_request]

</SectionTitle>

<SectionContent slot="content">

<OperationRequestBodyDescriptionSection slot="request-body-description">

</OperationRequestBodyDescriptionSection>

##### cursor [#operation-search_request_cursor]

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### groupName [#operation-search_responses_200_application-json_rewrittenfacetfilters_facetfilter_groupname]

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Indicates the value of a facet, if any, that the given facet is grouped under. This is only used for nested facets, for example, fieldName could be owner and groupName would be Spreadsheet if showing all owners for spreadsheets as a nested facet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

_Example:_

```
Spreadsheet
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

##### values [#operation-search_responses_200_application-json_rewrittenfacetfilters_facetfilter_values]

Within a single FacetFilter, the values are to be treated like an OR. For example, fieldName type with values [EQUALS Presentation, EQUALS Spreadsheet] means we want to show a document if it's a Presentation OR a Spreadsheet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>
